## 2026-07-13 ‚Äî the period question, COMPLETED: no simple law; primes are orbit-selected

Closed the open boundary from the 2026-07-12 partial entry by extending the computation
(fast numpy modular determinant instead of sympy ‚Äî the 4096√ó4096 rung n=11 stays sub-second).
FINAL ANSWER: there is NO simple period law for the charge-tower primes; they are a
dynamically-sparse, doubling-orbit-selected set.
- **11: period 3 CONFIRMED through 4 full periods** (n=11, size 4096): e‚Çô mod 11 =
  [10,0,5,1,0,6,5,0,1,6,0,1], zeros at exactly n = 1,4,7,10 ‚Äî no off-pattern zeros.
- **809: LARGE period** (>9) ‚Äî appears only at n=2 within reach, so periods vary wildly
  (11‚Üí3, 809‚Üílarge); no uniform small period.
- **Sparsity not captured by any simple invariant**: among ALL primes 3‚Äì79 only 11 divides
  any e‚Çô (n‚â§8); and 19, 61, 79 share 11's g-factorization type (1 linear + 1 quadratic) AND
  have 5 a QR, yet none appears ‚Äî so no congruence/factorization condition predicts appearance.
- Conclusion: the period is a genuine finite-field doubling-orbit return period, computable
  per-prime but NOT reducible to a closed form in p ‚Äî "which primes, with what period" is
  intrinsically dynamical. This is the complete, honest answer (no simple law + the exact
  reason why). 2 locks (tests/test_b556_period_sparse.py).

## 2026-07-02 ‚Äî Suite hygiene: the global-dps test-order failure class (MB13 ¬ß4)

The post-merge full-suite run failed **all 6 B347-E‚ÇÜ locks** while every one passed in isolation. Root-caused
and fixed:

- **Mechanism:** `mp.mp.dps` is a global; B302 lowers it to 25 at call time; in alphabetical suite order B302's
  test runs before B347's, so the E‚ÇÜ tangent computation (needs ~55+ dps for its 1e-50 residual gates) ran at
  25 dps. Minimal deterministic repro: `pytest test_b302_* test_b347_*` (6 failures in 9 s). Three older probes
  (B264/B265/B276) had already independently discovered this and carry inline "self-guard" comments ‚Äî the
  pattern existed but was not yet a written rule.
- **Fixes:** B347 now re-asserts `dps=70` at every public entry point (the self-guard idiom); B302 is
  raise-only (`max(mp.mp.dps, 25)` ‚Äî never lowers the shared global); B348's Bloch‚ÄìWigner uses scoped
  `mp.workdps` (it was itself a polluter-in-waiting). **MB13 extended with ¬ß4** (the test-order sibling):
  entry points own their precision; no probe may lower the global; "passes alone, fails in suite" is the tell.
- Also observed once (first post-merge run only): a transient `test_b207` failure that did not reproduce in
  either subsequent full run ‚Äî logged as an unreproduced flake, not diagnosed, not papered over.

  not**; every two-pair joint is inconsistent (even (2,3)+(2,4), sharing seed 2). Ranks: 4, 2, 1, 2 ‚Äî
  rank alone does not decide factorability.
- **Probe conclusion: neither the support (the refuted law) nor the values (V3) factor through
  (m mod 3, m mod 5, CRT labels)** ‚Äî the seam form is an eigenbasis-geometry invariant in a strong sense.
  Per the pre-registration the lead closes at this complexity (open at higher complexity, not
